nuxeo / Trainings
# Nuxeo Training - Forms and Views - Layouts
###What we want to do (1/3) ####At the end of the course: - Create a Book document with a custom creation form
###What we want to do (2/3) ####At the end of the course: - View the fields from the `Summary` tab
###What we want to do (3/3) ####At the end of the course: - Edit the fields from the custom `Edit`
### Layouts? Layouts : Declarative XML representation of a form or a view of a document - which metadata - how to display it (text field, text area, calendar ...) - form behaviour (validation, ...)
###Layouts for a document type A layout will edit/display a set of metadatas of a document ####Main layout - Creation layout
form displayed when creating the document (after having clicked on «New document»).
- Edit layout
form displayed when going on the edit tab of a document
- View layout
set of metadata displayed on the «summary» tab.
####Others - Summary layout
The whole summary tab. Display information about the documents and usually contains the view layout
- header layout
data displayed on top of the tabs when viewing a document in Nuxeo DM, by default the title and description
These layouts will use their default definition if not set in Studio
### Layouts in Nuxeo Studio Drag and drop field names from the right to the grid ### Widget? - Field presented to the user
A widget is a component that displays the information of one property on the document layout
- Edit or View mode
Ex: for a calendar, in view mode, the calendar widget displays the date value, in edit mode, it displays a calendar to select a value
- Validation
Default available validation: Required. Can define advanced validation in Java with Seam
- Different types (text, secret, datetime, ...) - Text
simple input text field
- Single User/group suggestion
a component that lists users and groups
- Document suggest
enables to select other existing documents
- Vocabulary and Chained vocabularies (See next chapter)
a list of values, on one level or 2 levels.
- Template
widgets made from a JSF XHTML file, by developers for getting any wanted behavior
###Widget properties - Label - Widget type
the proposed value depends on the type of the metadata)
- required
field has to be filled in the form
- Style, Style class: css information - Size, Max length, ...
properties that are leveraged by the HTML representation of the component

All the `Form layouts` will be display one after the others ####Common pattern Reusable form layout for a reusable schema
## Exercise
### Book form layout #### Form layout As we created a reusable schema `book`, it make sense to create a form layout for it. - Create a new formlayout called « bookLayout »  - Keep it empty for now #### Book layouts - For the `Book` creation, edit and view layouts  - Add the `heading` layout as an external layout - Add the new created `bookLayout` layout after - Disable all the local layouts
### ISBN Widget Definition - So let’s add ISBN widget to our `bookLayout`  - The field used for this widget will be book:isbn (that makes sense, right?)  - ISBN as label is really a good choice - The label doesn’t need to be translated - We want this field editable when we create the document, and then readonly when viewing or editing the document 
### Try out your changes - From the Admin Center in Nuxeo DM, update your Studio changes  - See that you can still create a new `Book` in a Folder or a Workspace  - Check that when creating it, you can enter the fields title, description and `bk:isbn` - When editing, the ISBN must be unmodifiable
### Some More Improvements... Add a widget for the `bk:author` for each layout
### Some More Improvements... - Add a new widget for the `bk:publicationDate` - This field is required and editable in creation layout  - Not displayed in edit layout  - Read-Only in view layout 
## Thank you!
